mysql> desc emp;
+-----------+-------------+------+-----+---------+-------+
| Field     | Type        | Null | Key | Default | Extra |
+-----------+-------------+------+-----+---------+-------+
| EMPNO     | int         | NO   | PRI | NULL    |       |
| ENAME     | varchar(12) | YES  |     | NULL    |       |
| GENDER    | char(1)     | YES  |     | NULL    |       |
| JOB       | varchar(20) | YES  |     | NULL    |       |
| MGR       | int         | YES  | MUL | NULL    |       |
| HIREDATE  | date        | YES  |     | NULL    |       |
| SAL       | int         | YES  |     | NULL    |       |
| COMM      | int         | YES  |     | NULL    |       |

mysql>
